                    const element = document.createElement('div');
                    element.innerHTML = html.trim();
                    
                    return element.firstChild;
                },
                
                // Mount component
                mount(instance, container) {
                    if (instance.mounted) {
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const component = this.components.get(instance.name);
                    
                    // Run before mount hook
                    if (this.hooks.beforeMount) {
                        this.hooks.beforeMount(instance, container);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's beforeMount hook
                    if (component.beforeMount) {
                        component.beforeMount(instance, container);
                    }
                    
                    // Append element to container
                    container.appendChild(instance.element);
                    instance.mounted = true;
                    
                    // Run after mount hook
                    if (this.hooks.afterMount) {
                        this.hooks.afterMount(instance, container);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's mounted hook
                    if (component.mounted) {
                        component.mounted(instance, container);
                    }
                    
                    // Emit mounted event
                    Uno.events.emit('component:mounted', instance);
                },
                
                // Unmount component
                unmount(instance) {
                    if (!instance.mounted) {
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const component = this.components.get(instance.name);
                    
                    // Run before unmount hook
                    if (this.hooks.beforeUnmount) {
                        this.hooks.beforeUnmount(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's beforeUnmount hook
                    if (component.beforeUnmount) {
                        component.beforeUnmount(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Remove element from DOM
                    if (instance.element && instance.element.parentNode) {
                        instance.element.parentNode.removeChild(instance.element);
                    }
                    instance.mounted = false;
                    
                    // Run after unmount hook
                    if (this.hooks.afterUnmount) {
                        this.hooks.afterUnmount(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's unmounted hook
                    if (component.unmounted) {
                        component.unmounted(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Emit unmounted event
                    Uno.events.emit('component:unmounted', instance);
                },
                
                // Destroy component
                destroy(instance) {
                    if (instance.destroyed) {
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const component = this.components.get(instance.name);
                    
                    // Unmount if mounted
                    if (instance.mounted) {
                        this.unmount(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Run before destroy hook
                    if (this.hooks.beforeDestroy) {
                        this.hooks.beforeDestroy(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's beforeDestroy hook
                    if (component.beforeDestroy) {
                        component.beforeDestroy(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Mark as destroyed
                    instance.destroyed = true;
                    
                    // Remove from instances
                    this.instances.delete(instance.id);
                    
                    // Run after destroy hook
                    if (this.hooks.afterDestroy) {
                        this.hooks.afterDestroy(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's destroyed hook
                    if (component.destroyed) {
                        component.destroyed(instance);
                    }
                    
                    // Emit destroyed event
                    Uno.events.emit('component:destroyed', instance);
                },
                
                // Update component
                update(instance, newState = {}) {
                    if (instance.destroyed) {
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    const component = this.components.get(instance.name);
                    
                    // Run before update hook
                    if (this.hooks.beforeUpdate) {
                        this.hooks.beforeUpdate(instance, newState);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's beforeUpdate hook
                    if (component.beforeUpdate) {
                        component.beforeUpdate(instance, newState);
                    }
                    
                    // Update state
                    Object.assign(instance.state, newState);
                    
                    // Re-render if mounted
                    if (instance.mounted) {
                        const newElement = this.render(instance);
                        
                        // Replace element in DOM
                        if (instance.element && instance.element.parentNode) {
                            instance.element.parentNode.replaceChild(newElement, instance.element);
                        }
                        
                        instance.element = newElement;
                    }
                    
                    // Run after update hook
                    if (this.hooks.afterUpdate) {
                        this.hooks.afterUpdate(instance, newState);
                    }
                    
                    // Run component's updated hook
                    if (component.updated) {
                        component.updated(instance, newState);
                    }
                    
                    // Emit updated event
                    Uno.events.emit('component:updated', instance);
                },
                
                // Mount all components with data-uno-component attribute
                mountAll() {
                    const elements = Uno.client.dom.findAll('[data-uno-component]');
                    
                    elements.forEach(element => {
                        const name = element.getAttribute('data-uno-component');
                        const props = JSON.parse(element.getAttribute('data-uno-props') || '{}');
                        
                        const instance = this.create(name, props);
                        this.mount(instance, element.parentNode);
                        
                        // Replace original element
                        if (element.parentNode) {
                            element.parentNode.replaceChild(instance.element, element);
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                // Get component instance by element
                getInstanceByElement(element) {
                    const id = element.getAttribute('data-uno-component');
                    return id ? this.instances.get(id) : null;
                }
            },
            
            // State management
            state: {
                // Initialize state management
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.state = options.initialState || {};
                    this.actions = options.actions || {};
                    this.mutations = options.mutations || {};
                    this.getters = options.getters || {};
                    this.modules = options.modules || {};
                    this.middlewares = options.middlewares || [];
                    this.subscribers = [];
                },
                
                // Get state
                getState(path) {
                    if (!path) {
                        return this.state;
                    }
                    
                    return path.split('.').reduce((obj, key) => {
                        return obj && obj[key];
                    }, this.state);
                },
                
                // Dispatch action
                async dispatch(action, payload) {
                    // Run middlewares
                    for (const middleware of this.middlewares) {
                        const result = await middleware(action, payload, this);
                        if (result === false) {
                            return;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Get action handler
                    const actionHandler = this.actions[action];
                    
                    if (!actionHandler) {
                        console.error(`Action "${action}" not found`);
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Execute action
                    await actionHandler({
                        state: this.state,
                        commit: this.commit.bind(this),
                        dispatch: this.dispatch.bind(this),
                        getters: this.getComputedGetters()
                    }, payload);
                    
                    // Notify subscribers
                    this.notifySubscribers();
                },
                
                // Commit mutation
                commit(mutation, payload) {
                    // Get mutation handler
                    const mutationHandler = this.mutations[mutation];
                    
                    if (!mutationHandler) {
                        console.error(`Mutation "${mutation}" not found`);
                        return;
                    }
                    
                    // Execute mutation
                    mutationHandler(this.state, payload);
                    
                    // Notify subscribers
                    this.notifySubscribers();
                },
                
                // Get computed getters
                getComputedGetters() {
                    const computed = {};
                    
                    for (const key in this.getters) {
                        computed[key] = this.getters[key](this.state);
                    }
                    
                    return computed;
                },
                
                // Subscribe to state changes
                subscribe(callback) {
                    this.subscribers.push(callback);
                    
                    // Return unsubscribe function
                    return () => {
                        const index = this.subscribers.indexOf(callback);
                        if (index !== -1) {
                            this.subscribers.splice(index, 1);
                        }
                    };
                },
                
                // Notify subscribers
                notifySubscribers() {
                    this.subscribers.forEach(callback => callback(this.state));
                },
                
                // Register module
                registerModule(name, module) {
                    this.modules[name] = module;
                    
                    // Initialize module state
                    if (module.state) {
                        this.state[name] = module.state;
                    }
                    
                    // Register module actions
                    if (module.actions) {
                        for (const key in module.actions) {
                            this.actions[`${name}/${key}`] = module.actions[key];
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Register module mutations
                    if (module.mutations) {
                        for (const key in module.mutations) {
                            this.mutations[`${name}/${key}`] = module.mutations[key];
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Register module getters
                    if (module.getters) {
                        for (const key in module.getters) {
                            this.getters[`${name}/${key}`] = (state) => {
                                return module.getters[key](state[name]);
                            };
                        }
                    }
                }
            },
            
            // Animation system
            animation: {
                // Initialize animation system
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.animations = new Map();
                    this.defaults = {
                        duration: 300,
                        easing: 'ease',
                        ...options
                    };
                },
                
                // Create animation
                create(element, keyframes, options = {}) {
                    const config = { ...this.defaults, ...options };
                    const animation = element.animate(keyframes, config);
                    
                    // Store animation
                    const id = Uno.utils.generateId();
                    this.animations.set(id, animation);
                    
                    // Remove from map when finished
                    animation.onfinish = () => {
                        this.animations.delete(id);
                    };
                    
                    return animation;
                },
                
                // Fade in element
                fadeIn(element, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { opacity: 0 },
                        { opacity: 1 }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Fade out element
                fadeOut(element, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { opacity: 1 },
                        { opacity: 0 }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Slide in element
                slideIn(element, direction = 'right', options = {}) {
                    let from, to;
                    
                    switch (direction) {
                        case 'up':
                            from = { transform: 'translateY(100%)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateY(0)' };
                            break;
                        case 'down':
                            from = { transform: 'translateY(-100%)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateY(0)' };
                            break;
                        case 'left':
                            from = { transform: 'translateX(100%)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateX(0)' };
                            break;
                        case 'right':
                        default:
                            from = { transform: 'translateX(-100%)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateX(0)' };
                            break;
                    }
                    
                    return this.create(element, [from, to], options);
                },
                
                // Slide out element
                slideOut(element, direction = 'right', options = {}) {
                    let from, to;
                    
                    switch (direction) {
                        case 'up':
                            from = { transform: 'translateY(0)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateY(-100%)' };
                            break;
                        case 'down':
                            from = { transform: 'translateY(0)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateY(100%)' };
                            break;
                        case 'left':
                            from = { transform: 'translateX(0)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateX(-100%)' };
                            break;
                        case 'right':
                        default:
                            from = { transform: 'translateX(0)' };
                            to = { transform: 'translateX(100%)' };
                            break;
                    }
                    
                    return this.create(element, [from, to], options);
                },
                
                // Scale element
                scale(element, fromScale = 0, toScale = 1, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { transform: `scale(${fromScale})` },
                        { transform: `scale(${toScale})` }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Rotate element
                rotate(element, fromAngle = 0, toAngle = 360, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { transform: `rotate(${fromAngle}deg)` },
                        { transform: `rotate(${toAngle}deg)` }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Bounce element
                bounce(element, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { transform: 'translateY(0)', easing: 'ease-in' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(-20%)', easing: 'ease-out' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(0)', easing: 'ease-in' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(-10%)', easing: 'ease-out' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(0)', easing: 'ease-in' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(-5%)', easing: 'ease-out' },
                        { transform: 'translateY(0)' }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Shake element
                shake(element, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { transform: 'translateX(0)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(-10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(-10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(-10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(10px)' },
                        { transform: 'translateX(0)' }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Pulse element
                pulse(element, options = {}) {
                    return this.create(element, [
                        { transform: 'scale(1)', opacity: 1 },
                        { transform: 'scale(1.05)', opacity: 0.7 },
                        { transform: 'scale(1)', opacity: 1 }
                    ], options);
                },
                
                // Stop animation
                stop(id) {
                    const animation = this.animations.get(id);
                    if (animation) {
                        animation.cancel();
                        this.animations.delete(id);
                    }
                },
                
                // Stop all animations
                stopAll() {
                    this.animations.forEach(animation => {
                        animation.cancel();
                    });
                    this.animations.clear();
                }
            },
            
            // Form handling
            forms: {
                // Initialize form handling
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.validators = options.validators || {};
                    this.serializers = options.serializers || {};
                    this.parsers = options.parsers || {};
                },
                
                // Validate form
                validate(form, rules) {
                    const errors = {};
                    let isValid = true;
                    
                    // Get form data
                    const data = this.serialize(form);
                    
                    // Validate each field
                    for (const field in rules) {
                        const fieldRules = rules[field];
                        const value = data[field];
                        const fieldErrors = [];
                        
                        // Check each rule
                        for (const rule of fieldRules) {
                            // Get validator
                            const validator = typeof rule === 'string' 
                                ? this.validators[rule] 
                                : rule;
                            
                            if (!validator) {
                                console.error(`Validator "${rule}" not found`);
                                continue;
                            }
                            
                            // Run validator
                            const result = validator(value, data);
                            
                            if (result !== true) {
                                fieldErrors.push(result);
                                isValid = false;
                            }
                        }
                        
                        // Add field errors if any
                        if (fieldErrors.length > 0) {
                            errors[field] = fieldErrors;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    return {
                        isValid,
                        errors,
                        data
                    };
                },
                
                // Serialize form
                serialize(form, options = {}) {
                    const data = {};
                    const elements = form.elements;
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                        const element = elements[i];
                        const name = element.name;
                        
                        if (!name) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        
                        // Get value based on element type
                        let value;
                        
                        if (element.type === 'checkbox') {
                            value = element.checked;
                        } else if (element.type === 'radio') {
                            if (element.checked) {
                                value = element.value;
                            } else {
                                continue;
                            }
                        } else if (element.tagName === 'SELECT') {
                            if (element.multiple) {
                                value = Array.from(element.selectedOptions).map(option => option.value);
                            } else {
                                value = element.value;
                            }
                        } else {
                            value = element.value;
                        }
                        
                        // Parse value if parser exists
                        if (this.parsers[element.type]) {
                            value = this.parsers[element.type](value);
                        }
                        
                        // Handle array notation (e.g., name="user[0].name")
                        if (name.includes('[') && name.includes(']')) {
                            this.setNestedValue(data, name, value);
                        } else {
                            // Handle multiple elements with the same name
                            if (data[name] !== undefined) {
                                if (Array.isArray(data[name])) {
                                    data[name].push(value);
                                } else {
                                    data[name] = [data[name], value];
                                }
                            } else {
                                data[name] = value;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    
                    return data;
                },
                
                // Set nested value
                setNestedValue(obj, path, value) {
                    const parts = path.split(/[\[\]]+/).filter(part => part !== '');
                    let current = obj;
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < parts.length - 1; i++) {
                        const part = parts[i];
                        
                        if (!current[part]) {
                            // Check if next part is a number (array index)
                            const nextPart = parts[i + 1];
                            if (!isNaN(nextPart)) {
                                current[part] = [];
                            } else {
                                current[part] = {};
                            }
                        }
                        
                        current = current[part];
                    }
                    
                    const lastPart = parts[parts.length - 1];
                    current[lastPart] = value;
                },
                
                // Populate form with data
                populate(form, data) {
                    const elements = form.elements;
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                        const element = elements[i];
                        const name = element.name;
                        
                        if (!name || data[name] === undefined) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        
                        const value = data[name];
                        
                        // Set value based on element type
                        if (element.type === 'checkbox') {
                            element.checked = !!value;
                        } else if (element.type === 'radio') {
                            element.checked = element.value === value;
                        } else if (element.tagName === 'SELECT') {
                            if (element.multiple) {
                                if (Array.isArray(value)) {
                                    Array.from(element.options).forEach(option => {
                                        option.selected = value.includes(option.value);
                                    });
                                }
                            } else {
                                element.value = value;
                            }
                        } else {
                            element.value = value;
                        }
                    }
                },
                
                // Clear form
                clear(form) {
                    form.reset();
                },
                
                // Add validator
                addValidator(name, validator) {
                    this.validators[name] = validator;
                },
                
                // Add serializer
                addSerializer(name, serializer) {
                    this.serializers[name] = serializer;
                },
                
                // Add parser
                addParser(name, parser) {
                    this.parsers[name] = parser;
                }
            },
            
            // Internationalization
            i18n: {
                // Initialize i18n
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.locale = options.locale || 'en';
                    this.fallbackLocale = options.fallbackLocale || 'en';
                    this.messages = options.messages || {};
                    this.dateTimeFormats = options.dateTimeFormats || {};
                    this.numberFormats = options.numberFormats || {};
                    this.modifiers = options.modifiers || {};
                },
                
                // Set locale
                setLocale(locale) {
                    this.locale = locale;
                    Uno.events.emit('i18n:locale-changed', locale);
                },
                
                // Get locale
                getLocale() {
                    return this.locale;
                },
                
                // Add messages
                    addMessages(locale, messages) {
                    if (!this.messages[locale]) {
                        this.messages[locale] = {};
                    }
                    
                    Object.assign(this.messages[locale], messages);
                },
                
                // Translate message
                t(key, params = {}, locale = this.locale) {
                    // Get message for locale
                    let message = this.getMessage(key, locale);
                    
                    // If not found, try fallback locale
                    if (!message && locale !== this.fallbackLocale) {
                        message = this.getMessage(key, this.fallbackLocale);
                    }
                    
                    // If still not found, return key
                    if (!message) {
                        return key;
                    }
                    
                    // Replace parameters
                    if (params && typeof message === 'string') {
                        for (const param in params) {
                            message = message.replace(`{${param}}`, params[param]);
                        }
                    }
                    
                    return message;
                },
                
                // Get message
                getMessage(key, locale) {
                    const messages = this.messages[locale];
                    
                    if (!messages) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    
                    // Handle nested keys (e.g., 'messages.welcome')
                    const parts = key.split('.');
                    let current = messages;
                    
                    for (const part of parts) {
                        if (current[part] === undefined) {
                            return null;
                        }
                        current = current[part];
                    }
                    
                    return current;
                },
                
                // Format date
                d(date, format = 'short', locale = this.locale) {
                    const formats = this.dateTimeFormats[locale];
                    
                    if (!formats || !formats[format]) {
                        return new Date(date).toLocaleDateString();
                    }
                    
                    return new Date(date).toLocaleDateString(locale, formats[format]);
                },
                
                // Format number
                n(number, format = 'decimal', locale = this.locale) {
                    const formats = this.numberFormats[locale];
                    
                    if (!formats || !formats[format]) {
                        return number.toLocaleString();
                    }
                    
                    return number.toLocaleString(locale, formats[format]);
                },
                
                // Format currency
                c(number, currency = 'USD', locale = this.locale) {
                    return number.toLocaleString(locale, {
                        style: 'currency',
                        currency
                    });
                },
                
                // Pluralize
                p(choice, choices, locale = this.locale) {
                    // Simple pluralization (in a real implementation, this would be more sophisticated)
                    if (typeof choices === 'string') {
                        choices = choices.split('|');
                    }
                    
                    const pluralRules = new Intl.PluralRules(locale);
                    const rule = pluralRules.select(choice);
                    
                    return choices[rule] || choices.other || choices[0];
                }
            },
            
            // Security
            security: {
                // Initialize security
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.csrfToken = options.csrfToken || null;
                    this.csrfHeaderName = options.csrfHeaderName || 'X-CSRF-TOKEN';
                    this.xssProtection = options.xssProtection !== false;
                    this.contentSecurityPolicy = options.contentSecurityPolicy || null;
                    this.secureCookies = options.secureCookies !== false;
                },
                
                // Set CSRF token
                setCsrfToken(token) {
                    this.csrfToken = token;
                },
                
                // Get CSRF token
                getCsrfToken() {
                    return this.csrfToken;
                },
                
                // Add CSRF token to headers
                addCsrfToken(headers = {}) {
                    if (this.csrfToken) {
                        headers[this.csrfHeaderName] = this.csrfToken;
                    }
                    return headers;
                },
                
                // Sanitize HTML
                sanitize(html) {
                    if (!this.xssProtection) {
                        return html;
                    }
                    
                    // Simple HTML sanitization (in a real implementation, this would be more sophisticated)
                    const div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.textContent = html;
                    return div.innerHTML;
                },
                
                // Escape HTML
                escape(html) {
                    const div = document.createElement('div');
                    div.textContent = html;
                    return div.innerHTML;
                },
                
                // Generate random token
                generateToken(length = 32) {
                    const chars = 'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789';
                    let token = '';
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < length; i++) {
                        token += chars.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * chars.length));
                    }
                    
                    return token;
                },
                
                // Hash string
                async hash(str) {
                    const encoder = new TextEncoder();
                    const data = encoder.encode(str);
                    const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
                    const hashArray = Array.from(new Uint8Array(hashBuffer));
                    
                    return hashArray.map(b => b.toString(16).padStart(2, '0')).join('');
                },
                
                // Compare strings with timing attack protection
                async compare(a, b) {
                    if (a.length !== b.length) {
                        return false;
                    }
                    
                    const encoder = new TextEncoder();
                    const dataA = encoder.encode(a);
                    const dataB = encoder.encode(b);
                    
                    const cryptoKey = await crypto.subtle.importKey(
                        'raw',
                        new Uint8Array(32),
                        { name: 'HMAC', hash: 'SHA-256' },
                        false,
                        ['verify']
                    );
                    
                    const signature = await crypto.subtle.sign('HMAC', cryptoKey, dataA);
                    return crypto.subtle.verify('HMAC', cryptoKey, signature, dataB);
                }
            },
            
            // Testing framework
            testing: {
                // Initialize testing framework
                init(options = {}) {
                    this.tests = [];
                    this.suites = [];
                    this.results = [];
                    this.reporters = options.reporters || [];
                },
                
                // Create test suite
                describe(name, callback) {
                    const suite = {
                        name,
                        tests: [],
                        beforeAll: null,
                        afterAll: null,
                        beforeEach: null,
                        afterEach: null
                    };
                    
                    // Store current suite
                    const currentSuite = this.currentSuite;
                    this.currentSuite = suite;
                    
                    // Execute callback to add tests
                    callback();
                    
                    // Restore previous suite
                    this.currentSuite = currentSuite;
                    
                    // Add to suites
                    this.suites.push(suite);
                    
                    return suite;
                },
                
                // Create test
                it(name, callback) {
                    if (!this.currentSuite) {
                        throw new Error('Test must be inside a describe block');
                    }
                    
                    const test = {
                        name,
                        callback,
                        timeout: 5000
                    };
                    
                    this.currentSuite.tests.push(test);
                    
                    return test;
                },
                
                // Set before all hook
                beforeAll(callback) {
                    if (!this.currentSuite) {
                        throw new Error('beforeAll must be inside a describe block');
                    }
                    
                    this.currentSuite.beforeAll = callback;
                },
                
                // Set after all hook
                afterAll(callback) {
                    if (!this.currentSuite) {
                        throw new Error('afterAll must be inside a describe block');
                    }
                    
                    this.currentSuite.afterAll = callback;
                },
                
                // Set before each hook
                beforeEach(callback) {
                    if (!this.currentSuite) {
                        throw new Error('beforeEach must be inside a describe block');
                    }
                    
                    this.currentSuite.beforeEach = callback;
                },
                
                // Set after each hook
                afterEach(callback) {
                    if (!this.currentSuite) {
                        throw new Error('afterEach must be inside a describe block');
                    }
                    
                    this.currentSuite.afterEach = callback;
                },
                
                // Run all tests
                async run() {
                    this.results = [];
                    
                    // Notify reporters
                    this.notifyReporters('start', { suites: this.suites });
                    
                    // Run each suite
                    for (const suite of this.suites) {
                        // Notify reporters
                        this.notifyReporters('suiteStart', { suite });
                        
                        // Run before all hook
                        if (suite.beforeAll) {
                            await suite.beforeAll();
                        }
                        
                        // Run each test
                        for (const test of suite.tests) {
                            // Notify reporters
                            this.notifyReporters('testStart', { suite, test });
                            
                            // Run before each hook
                            if (suite.beforeEach) {
                                await suite.beforeEach();
                            }
                            
                            // Run test
                            const result = {
                                suite: suite.name,
                                test: test.name,
                                passed: false,
                                error: null,
                                duration: 0
                            };
                            
                            const startTime = Date.now();
                            
                            try {
                                // Set timeout
                                const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) => {
                                    setTimeout(() => reject(new Error(`Test timed out after ${test.timeout}ms`)), test.timeout);
                                });
                                
                                // Run test
                                await Promise.race([test.callback(), timeoutPromise]);
                                
                                result.passed = true;
                            } catch (error) {
                                result.error = error.message;
                            }
                            
                            result.duration = Date.now() - startTime;
                            
                            // Run after each hook
                            if (suite.afterEach) {
                                await suite.afterEach();
                            }
                            
                            // Add to results
                            this.results.push(result);
                            
                            // Notify reporters
                            this.notifyReporters('testEnd', { suite, test, result });
                        }
                        
                        // Run after all hook
                        if (suite.afterAll) {
                            await suite.afterAll();
                        }
                        
                        // Notify reporters
                        this.notifyReporters('suiteEnd', { suite });
                    }
                    
                    // Calculate summary
                    const summary = {
                        total: this.results.length,
                        passed: this.results.filter(r => r.passed).length,
                        failed: this.results.filter(r => !r.passed).length,
                        duration: this.results.reduce((total, r) => total + r.duration, 0)
                    };
                    
                    // Notify reporters
                    this.notifyReporters('end', { results: this.results, summary });
                    
                    return summary;
                },
                
                // Add reporter
                addReporter(reporter) {
                    this.reporters.push(reporter);
                },
                
                // Notify reporters
                notifyReporters(event, data) {
                    this.reporters.forEach(reporter => {
                        if (typeof reporter[event] === 'function') {
                            reporter[event](data);
                        }
                    });
                },
                
                // Assert functions
                assert: {
                    // Assert that value is true
                    isTrue(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be true`) {
                        if (value !== true) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is false
                    isFalse(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be false`) {
                        if (value !== false) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that values are equal
                    equal(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to equal ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual !== expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that values are not equal
                    notEqual(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to not equal ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual === expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is null
                    isNull(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be null`) {
                        if (value !== null) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is not null
                    isNotNull(value, message = `Expected ${value} to not be null`) {
                        if (value === null) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is undefined
                    isUndefined(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be undefined`) {
                        if (value !== undefined) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is not undefined
                    isNotUndefined(value, message = `Expected ${value} to not be undefined`) {
                        if (value === undefined) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is defined
                    isDefined(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be defined`) {
                        if (value === undefined) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is NaN
                    isNaN(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be NaN`) {
                        if (!Number.isNaN(value)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is not NaN
                    isNotNaN(value, message = `Expected ${value} to not be NaN`) {
                        if (Number.isNaN(value)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is greater than expected
                    greaterThan(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to be greater than ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual <= expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is less than expected
                    lessThan(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to be less than ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual >= expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is greater than or equal to expected
                    greaterThanOrEqual(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to be greater than or equal to ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual < expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is less than or equal to expected
                    lessThanOrEqual(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to be less than or equal to ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual > expected) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value contains expected
                    contains(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to contain ${expected}`) {
                        if (!actual.includes(expected)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value does not contain expected
                    notContains(actual, expected, message = `Expected ${actual} to not contain ${expected}`) {
                        if (actual.includes(expected)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value matches regex
                    matches(actual, regex, message = `Expected ${actual} to match ${regex}`) {
                        if (!regex.test(actual)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value does not match regex
                    notMatches(actual, regex, message = `Expected ${actual} to not match ${regex}`) {
                        if (regex.test(actual)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that function throws
                    throws(fn, message = `Expected function to throw`) {
                        let threw = false;
                        
                        try {
                            fn();
                        } catch (e) {
                            threw = true;
                        }
                        
                        if (!threw) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that function does not throw
                    doesNotThrow(fn, message = `Expected function to not throw`) {
                        try {
                            fn();
                        } catch (e) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is an instance of constructor
                    isInstanceOf(value, constructor, message = `Expected ${value} to be an instance of ${constructor.name}`) {
                        if (!(value instanceof constructor)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is not an instance of constructor
                    isNotInstanceOf(value, constructor, message = `Expected ${value} to not be an instance of ${constructor.name}`) {
                        if (value instanceof constructor) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value has property
                    hasProperty(value, property, message = `Expected ${value} to have property ${property}`) {
                        if (!(property in value)) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value does not have property
                    doesNotHaveProperty(value, property, message = `Expected ${value} to not have property ${property}`) {
                        if (property in value) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value has method
                    hasMethod(value, method, message = `Expected ${value} to have method ${method}`) {
                        if (typeof value[method] !== 'function') {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value does not have method
                    doesNotHaveMethod(value, method, message = `Expected ${value} to not have method ${method}`) {
                        if (typeof value[method] === 'function') {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that array has length
                    hasLength(value, length, message = `Expected array to have length ${length}`) {
                        if (value.length !== length) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is empty
                    isEmpty(value, message = `Expected ${value} to be empty`) {
                        if (value.length !== 0) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Assert that value is not empty
                    isNotEmpty(value, message = `Expected ${value} to not be empty`) {
                        if (value.length === 0) {
                            throw new Error(message);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        },
        
        // Server-side functionality
        server: {
            // Initialize server
            init(options = {}) {
                this.port = options.port || 3000;
                this.host = options.host || 'localhost';
                this.routes = new Map();
                this.middlewares = [];
                this.static = options.static || {};
                this.views = options.views || {};
                this.engine = options.engine || null;
                this.session = options.session || {};
                this.csrf = options.csrf || {};
                this.rateLimit = options.rateLimit || {};
                this.cors = options.cors || {};
                this.helmet = options.helmet || {};
                this.compression = options.compression || {};
                this.https = options.https || {};
                this.websockets = options.websockets || {};
                this.database = options.database || {};
                this.auth = options.auth || {};
                this.logger = options.logger || {};
                
                // Initialize HTTP server
                this.http = require('http');
                this.https = require('https');
                this.fs = require('fs');
                this.path = require('path');
                this.url = require('url');
                this.querystring = require('querystring');
                this.crypto = require('crypto');
                
                // Create server
                if (this.https.enabled) {
                    this.server = this.https.createServer(
                        {
                            key: this.fs.readFileSync(this.https.key),
                            cert: this.fs.readFileSync(this.https.cert)
                        },
                        this.handleRequest.bind(this)
                    );
                } else {
                    this.server = this.http.createServer(this.handleRequest.bind(this));
                }
                
                // Initialize WebSocket server
                if (this.websockets.enabled) {
                    const WebSocket = require('ws');
                    this.wsServer = new WebSocket.Server({ server: this.server });
                    
                    this.wsServer.on('connection', (ws, req) => {
                        this.handleWebSocketConnection(ws, req);
                    });
                }
                
                // Start server
                this.server.listen(this.port, this.host, () => {
                    console.log(`Server running at http${this.https.enabled ? 's' : ''}://${this.host}:${this.port}`);
                });
            },
            
            // Handle HTTP request
            async handleRequest(req, res) {
                try {
                    // Parse URL
                    const parsedUrl = this.url.parse(req.url, true);
                    const pathname = parsedUrl.pathname;
                    const query = parsedUrl.query;
                    
                    // Parse method
                    const method = req.method.toLowerCase();
                    
                    // Parse body
                    let body = '';
                    req.on('data', chunk => {
                        body += chunk.toString();
                    });
                    
                    req.on('end', async () => {
                        try {
                            // Parse body based on content type
                            const contentType = req.headers['content-type'] || '';
                            
                            if (contentType.includes('application/json')) {
                                try {
                                    body = JSON.parse(body);
                                } catch (e) {
                                    body = {};
                                }
                            } else if (contentType.includes('application/x-www-form-urlencoded')) {
                                body = this.querystring.parse(body);
                            }
                            
                            // Create request object
                            const request = {
                                method,
                                url: req.url,
                                pathname,
                                query,
                                headers: req.headers,
                                body,
                                params: {},
                                cookies: this.parseCookies(req.headers.cookie || ''),
                                session: {},
                                user: null
                            };
                            
                            // Create response object
                            const response = {
                                status: 200,
                                headers: {},
                                cookies: {},
                                body: null,
                                sent: false,
                                
                                // Set status
                                status(code) {
                                    this.status = code;
                                    return this;
                                },
                                
                                // Set header
                                set(name, value) {
                                    this.headers[name] = value;
                                    return this;
                                },
                                
                                // Set cookie
                                cookie(name, value, options = {}) {
                                    this.cookies[name] = { value, options };
                                    return this;
                                },
                                
                                // Send response
                                send(data) {
                                    if (this.sent) {
                                        return;
                                    }
                                    
                                    this.sent = true;
                                    this.body = data;
                                    
                                    // Set headers
                                    for (const name in this.headers) {
                                        res.setHeader(name, this.headers[name]);
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Set cookies
                                    for (const name in this.cookies) {
                                        const { value, options } = this.cookies[name];
                                        let cookie = `${name}=${value}`;
                                        
                                        if (options.maxAge) {
                                            cookie += `; Max-Age=${options.maxAge}`;
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.expires) {
                                            cookie += `; Expires=${options.expires.toUTCString()}`;
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.path) {
                                            cookie += `; Path=${options.path}`;
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.domain) {
                                            cookie += `; Domain=${options.domain}`;
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.secure) {
                                            cookie += '; Secure';
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.httpOnly) {
                                            cookie += '; HttpOnly';
                                        }
                                        
                                        if (options.sameSite) {
                                            cookie += `; SameSite=${options.sameSite}`;
                                        }
                                        
                                        res.setHeader('Set-Cookie', cookie);
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Send status
                                    res.statusCode = this.status;
                                    
                                    // Send body
                                    if (typeof data === 'object') {
                                        res.setHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
                                        res.end(JSON.stringify(data));
                                    } else {
                                        res.end(data);
                                    }
                                },
                                
                                // Redirect
                                redirect(url, status = 302) {
                                    this.status(status).set('Location', url).send();
                                },
                                
                                // Render template
                                render(template, data = {}) {
                                    // Get template engine
                                    const engine = this.engine || Uno.server.views.engine;
                                    
                                    if (!engine) {
                                        return this.status(500).send('Template engine not configured');
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Render template
                                    const html = engine(template, data);
                                    
                                    // Send response
                                    this.set('Content-Type', 'text/html').send(html);
                                }
                            };
                            
                            // Run middlewares
                            let middlewareIndex = 0;
                            
                            const next = async () => {
                                if (middlewareIndex >= this.middlewares.length) {
                                    // Find route
                                    const route = this.findRoute(method, pathname);
                                    
                                    if (route) {
                                        // Extract params
                                        request.params = this.extractParams(route.path, pathname);
                                        
                                        // Run route handler
                                        await route.handler(request, response);
                                    } else {
                                        // Try to serve static file
                                        const staticFile = this.serveStaticFile(pathname);
                                        
                                        if (staticFile) {
                                            const { content, type } = staticFile;
                                            response.set('Content-Type', type).send(content);
                                        } else {
                                            // 404
                                            response.status(404).send('Not Found');
                                        }
                                    }
                                    
                                    return;
                                }
                                
                                const middleware = this.middlewares[middlewareIndex++];
                                await middleware(request, response, next);
                            };
                            
                            await next();
                        } catch (error) {
                            console.error(error);
                            res.statusCode = 500;
                            res.end('Internal Server Error');
                        }
                    });
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error(error);
                    res.statusCode = 500;
                    res.end('Internal Server Error');
                }
            },
            
            // Handle WebSocket connection
            handleWebSocketConnection(ws, req) {
                // Parse URL
                const parsedUrl = this.url.parse(req.url, true);
                const pathname = parsedUrl.pathname;
                const query = parsedUrl.query;
                
                // Create connection object
                const connection = {
                    ws,
                    req,
                    url: req.url,
                    pathname,
                    query,
                    params: {},
                    data: {},
                    rooms: new Set(),
                    
                    // Send message
                    send(data) {
                        this.ws.send(typeof data === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(data) : data);
                    },
                    
                    // Join room
                    join(room) {
                        this.rooms.add(room);
                        
                        if (!Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room]) {
                            Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room] = new Set();
                        }
                        
                        Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room].add(this);
                    },
                    
                    // Leave room
                    leave(room) {
                        this.rooms.delete(room);
                        
                        if (Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room]) {
                            Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room].delete(this);
                            
                            if (Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room].size === 0) {
                                delete Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room];
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Broadcast to room
                    broadcast(room, data) {
                        if (Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room]) {
                            Uno.server.websockets.rooms[room].forEach(connection => {
                                if (connection !== this) {
                                    connection.send(data);
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    },
                    
                    // Close connection
                    close() {
                        this.ws.close();
                    }
                };
                
                // Find WebSocket route
                const route = this.findWebSocketRoute(pathname);
                
                if (route) {
                    // Extract params
                    connection.params = this.extractParams(route.path, pathname);
                    
                    // Run route handler
                    route.handler(connection);
                } else {
                    // Close connection
                    ws.close();
                }
                
                // Handle close
                ws.on('close', () => {
                    // Leave all rooms
                    connection.rooms.forEach(room => {
                        connection.leave(room);
                    });
                });
            },
            
            // Find route
            findRoute(method, pathname) {
                for (const [path, route] of this.routes) {
                    if (route.method === method && this.matchPath(path, pathname)) {
                        return { path, handler: route.handler };
                    }
                }
                
                return null;
            },
            
            // Find WebSocket route
            findWebSocketRoute(pathname) {
                for (const [path, handler] of this.websockets.routes || []) {
                    if (this.matchPath(path, pathname)) {
                        return { path, handler };
                    }
                }
                
                return null;
            },
            
            // Match path
            matchPath(route, pathname) {
                // Convert route to regex
                const regex = new RegExp('^' + route.replace(/:[^/]+/g, '([^/]+)') + '$');
                return regex.test(pathname);
            },
            
            // Extract params
            extractParams(route, pathname) {
                const params = {};
                
                // Convert route to regex
                const regex = new RegExp('^' + route.replace(/:[^/]+/g, '([^/]+)') + '$');
                const match = pathname.match(regex);
                
                if (match) {
                    // Get param names
                    const paramNames = route.match(/:[^/]+/g) || [];
                    
                    // Extract params
                    paramNames.forEach((name, index) => {
                        params[name.substring(1)] = match[index + 1];
                    });
                }
                
                return params;
            },
            
            // Parse cookies
            parseCookies(cookieString) {
                const cookies = {};
                
                if (cookieString) {
                    cookieString.split(';').forEach(cookie => {
                        const parts = cookie.trim().split('=');
                        const name = parts[0];
                        const value = parts[1];
                        
                        cookies[name] = value;
                    });
                }
                
                return cookies;
            },
            
            // Serve static file
            serveStaticFile(pathname) {
                // Check if static is enabled
                if (!this.static.enabled) {
                    return null;
                }
                
                // Get file path
                const filePath = this.path.join(this.static.root, pathname);
                
                // Check if file exists
                if (!this.fs.existsSync(filePath) || !this.fs.statSync(filePath).isFile()) {
                    return null;
                }
                
                // Get file extension
                const ext = this.path.extname(filePath).substring(1);
                
                // Get MIME type
                const mimeType = this.static.mimeTypes[ext] || 'application/octet-stream';
                
                // Read file
                const content = this.fs.readFileSync(filePath);
                
                return { content, type: mimeType };
            },
            
            // Add route
            add(method, path, handler) {
                this.routes.set(path, { method, handler });
            },
            
            // Add middleware
            use(middleware) {
                this.middlewares.push(middleware);
            },
            
            // Add WebSocket route
            ws(path, handler) {
                if (!this.websockets.routes) {
                    this.websockets.routes = [];
                }
                
                this.websockets.routes.push([path, handler]);
            },
            
            // Initialize rooms
            initRooms() {
                this.websockets.rooms = {};
            },
            
            // Broadcast to all connections
            broadcast(data) {
                if (this.wsServer) {
                    this.wsServer.clients.forEach(client => {
                        if (client.readyState === 1) { // WebSocket.OPEN
                            client.send(typeof data === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(data) : data);
                        }
                    });
                }
            },
            
            // Broadcast to room
            broadcastToRoom(room, data) {
                if (this.websockets.rooms[room]) {
                    this.websockets.rooms[room].forEach(connection => {
                        connection.send(data);
                    });
                }
            }
        },
        
        // Plugin system
        plugins: {
            // Initialize plugin system
            init() {
                this.plugins = new Map();
                this.hooks = {
                    beforeInit: [],
                    afterInit: [],
                    beforeCreate: [],
                    afterCreate: [],
                    beforeMount: [],
                    afterMount: [],
                    beforeUpdate: [],
                    afterUpdate: [],
                    beforeDestroy: [],
                    afterDestroy: []
                };
            },
            
            // Register plugin
            register(name, plugin) {
                // Check if plugin is already registered
                if (this.plugins.has(name)) {
                    console.warn(`Plugin "${name}" is already registered`);
                    return;
                }
                
                // Store plugin
                this.plugins.set(name, plugin);
                
                // Run plugin install
                if (typeof plugin.install === 'function') {
                    plugin.install(Uno);
                }
                
                // Register hooks
                if (plugin.hooks) {
                    for (const hook in plugin.hooks) {
                        if (this.hooks[hook]) {
                            this.hooks[hook].push(plugin.hooks[hook]);
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // Emit plugin registered event
                Uno.events.emit('plugin:registered', { name, plugin });
            },
            
            // Unregister plugin
            unregister(name) {
                // Check if plugin is registered
                if (!this.plugins.has(name)) {
                    console.warn(`Plugin "${name}" is not registered`);
                    return;
                }
                
                // Get plugin
                const plugin = this.plugins.get(name);
                
                // Run plugin uninstall
                if (typeof plugin.uninstall === 'function') {
                    plugin.uninstall(Uno);
                }
                
                // Remove hooks
                if (plugin.hooks) {
                    for (const hook in plugin.hooks) {
                        if (this.hooks[hook]) {
                            const index = this.hooks[hook].indexOf(plugin.hooks[hook]);
                            if (index !== -1) {
                                this.hooks[hook].splice(index, 1);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                // Remove plugin
                this.plugins.delete(name);
                
                // Emit plugin unregistered event
                Uno.events.emit('plugin:unregistered', { name });
            },
            
            // Get plugin
            get(name) {
                return this.plugins.get(name);
            },
            
            // Check if plugin is registered
            has(name) {
                return this.plugins.has(name);
            },
            
            // List all plugins
            list() {
                return Array.from(this.plugins.keys());
            },
            
            // Run hook
            async runHook(hook, ...args) {
                if (!this.hooks[hook]) {
                    return;
                }
                
                for (const handler of this.hooks[hook]) {
                    await handler(...args);
                }
            }
        }
    };

    // Expose Uno to global
    if (typeof module !== 'undefined' && module.exports) {
        module.exports = Uno;
    } else {
        global.Uno = Uno;
    }
})(typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window : global);
